Question Name: SosyalIntro
===========================
Type: Open-end (single line)
Required: YES
Min Characters: 10
Max Characters: 10
---------------------------

[Pre-Skips]:
Pre-Skip: Skip from SosyalIntro to NEXT QUESTION if Yontem<>3

[Question]:
Merhaba! 
İnovatif Ürün araştırması için hazırladığımız anketimize katılmak üzeresiniz. Anketimiz yaklaşık 10 dakika sürecek ve tüm cevaplarınız gizli tutulacaktır. 
Düşünceleriniz ve vaktiniz bizim için çok değerli! Şimdiden katılımınız için teşekkür ederiz. Anket bitimindeki hediyenizi teslim edebilmemiz için lütfen telefon numaranızı başında sıfır olmadan paylaşınız.
Telefon Numarası: (0)


[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

var valIntro=SSI_GetValue('SosyalIntro');
var GsmExp = /^(?!0)[0-9]{10}?$/;
if ( (valIntro.length > 0 && GsmExp.test(valIntro) == false) || (valIntro.length < 10) || (valIntro.substring(0,1)!='5') )
{
strErrorMessage = "Lütfen cep telefonu numarasını kontrol ediniz.";
document.mainform['SosyalIntro'].focus();
}

Type: Select (Radio Button)
Required: YES
---------------------------

[Pre-Skips]:
Pre-Skip: Skip from AramaDurumu to NEXT QUESTION if Yontem<>2

[Header 1]:
Arama Sayisi: [% LoopIteration() %] . Arama

[Question]:
Arama Durumu

[Response Options]:
List Name: AramaDurumuList
Type: Predefined

1	Telefon cevap verdi
2	Red etti [Respondent Specify]
3	Telefon cevap vermiyor
4	Ulaşılamıyor mesajı
5	Telefon meşgul
6	Hat bozuk/Kullanılmayan
7	Kota Dışı [Respondent Specify]
8	Denek şu an müsait değil
9	Randevu verdi (yazınız gün-saat) [Respondent Specify]
10	Çağrı merkezinden ötürü ulaşılamıyor
11	Mail ile katılmayı tercih ediyor [Respondent Specify]
12	Diğer (yazınız) [Respondent Specify]
13	Öyle biri yok
14	Görüşmeci Tekrar Aranmak istemiyor

[Post-Skips]:
Post-Skip: Skip from AramaDurumu to NEXT LOOP ITERATION if Begin Unverified Perl

End Unverified

	my @arr=split(/-/,LISTLABEL("GRUPYASList",$i));
    if (@arr[1]!="")
    {
		for (my $age=@arr[0]; $age<=@arr[1]; $age++)

// Verification functions
var verifySelectQuestion = function(question, minimum) {
minimum = minimum || 0;
var list = $('input[name="hid_list_' + question + '"]').val().split(',');
if (!$('#' + question + '_' + list[0]).is('[type="checkbox"]')) {
if (!SSI_GetValue(question)) {
addMissingAnswerErrorMessageToQuestion(question);
addErrorVariableHighlight($('#' + question));
}
}
else {
if (minimum) {
var checks = 0;
list.forEach(function(item){
checks += SSI_GetValue(question + '_' + item);
});
if (checks < minimum) {
addMinimumChecksErrorMessageToQuestion(question, minimum);
}
}
}
}
var verifyNumericQuestion = function(question) {
if (!$('#' + question).val().trim().length) {
addMissingAnswerErrorMessageToQuestion(question);
addErrorVariableHighlight($('#' + question));
}
}
var verifyOpenEndQuestion = function(question, minimum) {
minimum = minimum || 1;
if ($('#' + question).val().trim().length < minimum) {
addMinimumCharactersErrorMessageToQuestion(question, minimum);
addErrorVariableHighlight($('#' + question));
}
}
var verifyConstantSumQuestion = function(question) {
verifyConstantSumOrRankingQuestion(question, function(item){
return $('#' + question + '_' + item).val().trim().length;
});
}
var verifyRankingQuestion = function(question) {
if ($('#' + question + '_div').find('select, .ui-sortable').length) {
verifyConstantSumOrRankingQuestion(question, function(item){
return SSI_GetValue(question + '_' + item);
});
}
else {
verifyConstantSumOrRankingQuestion(question, function(item){
return $('#' + question + '_' + item).val().trim().length;
});
}
}
var verifyConstantSumOrRankingQuestion = function(question, isAnsweredFunction) {
var answered = false;
var list = $('input[name="hid_list_' + question + '"]').val().split(',');
for (var i = 0; i < list.length; i++) {
if (isAnsweredFunction(list[i])) {
answered = true;
break;
}
}
if (!answered) {
addMissingAnswerErrorMessageToQuestion(question);
addErrorVariableHighlightToDescendents($('#' + question + '_div'));
}
}
var verifySemanticDiffQuestion = function(question) {
var answered = true;
var usesSliders = $('#' + question + '_div .ui-slider').length > 0;
var list = $('input[name="hid_list_' + question + '"]').val().split(',');
list.forEach(function(item){
if (!SSI_GetValue(question + '_' + item)) {
answered = false;
if (usesSliders) {
addErrorVariableHighlight($('#' + question + '_' + item));
}
else {
addGridRowErrorVariableHighlight($('input[name="' + question + '_' + item + '"]'));
}
}
});
if (!answered) {
addMissingAnswerErrorMessageToQuestion(question);
}
}
var verifyGridQuestion = function(question, minimums) {
minimums = minimums || {};
var grid = SSI_GetGridQuestionSettings(question);
var rowsList = grid.rows;
var columnsList = grid.columns;
// Row-oriented
if (grid.orientation == 'row') {
for (var r = 0; r < rowsList.length; r++) {
var row = rowsList[r];
var constantSumOrRanking = grid.variables[r].variableType == 'constant sum' || grid.variables[r].variableType == 'ranking';
var firstRadioInput = $('#' + question + '_r' + row + '_' + columnsList[0] + '[type="radio"]');
var firstNonRadioInput = $('#' + question + '_r' + row + '_c' + columnsList[0]);
// Radio buttons
if ($(firstRadioInput).length) {
verifyGridRadioRow(question, row, columnsList);
}
// Checkboxes
else if ($(firstNonRadioInput).is('[type="checkbox"]')) {
verifyGridCheckboxRow(question, row, columnsList, minimums[row]);
}
// Select comboboxes, numeric, open-ends
else if (!constantSumOrRanking) {
// Select comboboxes
if ($(firstNonRadioInput).is('select')) {
verifyGridSelectComboboxRow(question, row, columnsList);
}
// Numerics
else if ($(firstNonRadioInput).is('[type="tel"]')) {
verifyGridNumericRow(question, row, columnsList);
}
// Open-ends
else {
verifyGridOpenEndRow(question, row, columnsList, minimums[row]);
}
}
// Ranking comboboxes
else if ($(firstNonRadioInput).is('select')) {
verifyGridRankingComboboxRow(question, row, columnsList);
}
// Constant sum, ranking
else {
verifyGridConstantSumOrRankingRow(question, row, columnsList);
}
}
}
// Column-oriented
else {
for (var c = 0; c < columnsList.length; c++) {
var column = columnsList[c];
var constantSumOrRanking = grid.variables[c].variableType == 'constant sum' || grid.variables[c].variableType == 'ranking';
var firstRadioInput = $('#' + question + '_c' + column + '_' + rowsList[0] + '[type="radio"]');
var firstNonRadioInput = $('#' + question + '_r' + rowsList[0] + '_c' + column);
// Radio buttons
if ($(firstRadioInput).length) {
verifyGridRadioColumn(question, column, rowsList);
}
// Checkboxes
else if ($(firstNonRadioInput).is('[type="checkbox"]')) {
verifyGridCheckboxColumn(question, column, rowsList, minimums[column]);
}
// Select comboboxes, numeric, open-ends
else if (!constantSumOrRanking) {
// Select comboboxes
if ($(firstNonRadioInput).is('select')) {
verifyGridSelectComboboxColumn(question, column, rowsList);
}
// Numerics
else if ($(firstNonRadioInput).is('[type="tel"]')) {
verifyGridNumericColumn(question, column, rowsList);
}
// Open-ends
else {
verifyGridOpenEndColumn(question, column, rowsList, minimums[column]);
}
}
// Ranking comboboxes
else if ($(firstNonRadioInput).is('select')) {
verifyGridRankingComboboxColumn(question, column, rowsList);
}
// Constant sum, ranking
else {
verifyGridConstantSumOrRankingColumn(question, column, rowsList);
}
}
}
}
var verifyGridRadioRow = function(question, row, columnsList) {
if (!SSI_GetValue(question + '_r' + row)) {
addMissingAnswerErrorMessageToQuestion(question);
addGridRowErrorVariableHighlight('#' + question + '_r' + row + '_' + columnsList[0]);
}
}
var verifyGridRadioColumn = function(question, column, rowsList) {
if (!SSI_GetValue(question + '_c' + column)) {
addMissingAnswerErrorMessageToQuestion(question);
addGridColumnErrorVariableHighlight('#' + question + '_c' + column + '_' + rowsList[0]);
}
}

});

}
}
}

});

var verifyGridOpenEndRow = function(question, row, columnsList, minimum) {
minimum = getOpenEndMinimumOrDefault(minimum);
if (minimum) {
var foundError = false;
columnsList.forEach(function(column){
var variable = question + '_r' + row + '_c' + column;
if ($('#' + variable).val().trim().length < minimum) {
foundError = true;
addErrorVariableHighlight('#' + variable);
}
});
if (foundError) {
addMinimumCharactersErrorMessageToQuestion(question, minimum);
}
}
}

var verifyFreeFormatQuestion = function(question, minimums) {
minimums = minimums || {};
var freeFormat = SSI_GetFreeFormatQuestionSettings(question);
freeFormat.variables.forEach(function(variable){
switch (variable.variableType) {
// Radio, combo variable
case 'radio':
case 'select':
if (!SSI_GetValue(question + '_' + variable.name)) {
addMissingAnswerErrorMessageToQuestion(question);
addErrorVariableHighlight($('#' + question + '_' + variable.name));
}
break;
// Checkbox variable
case 'checkbox':
var minimum = minimums[variable.name] || 0;
if (minimum) {
var checks = 0;
$('input[type="checkbox"][name^="' + question + '_' + variable.name + '_"]').each(function(){
checks += SSI_GetValue(this.name);
});
if (checks < minimum) {
addMinimumChecksErrorMessageToQuestion(question, minimum);
}
}
break;
// Numeric variable
case 'numeric':
var element = $('#' + question + '_' + variable.name);
if (!element.val().trim().length) {
addMissingAnswerErrorMessageToQuestion(question);
addErrorVariableHighlight(element);
}
break;
// Text variable
case 'text':
var minimum = getOpenEndMinimumOrDefault(minimums[variable.name]);
if (minimum) {
var element = $('#' + question + '_' + variable.name);
if (element.val().trim().length < minimum) {
addMinimumCharactersErrorMessageToQuestion(question, minimum);
addErrorVariableHighlight(element);
}
}
break;
}
});
};
var getOpenEndMinimumOrDefault = function(minimum) {
return minimum == 0 || minimum ? minimum : 1;
};
// Error state functions
var addMissingAnswerErrorMessageToQuestion = function(question) {
if (!$('#' + question + '_div .missing_answer_branching').length) {
addErrorMessageToQuestion(question, GLOBAL_SAWTOOTH_[% QUESTIONNAME() %]_SETTINGS.errorMessageSettings.missingAnswer, true);
}
};
var addMinimumChecksErrorMessageToQuestion = function(question, minimumChecks) {
addErrorMessageToQuestion(question, GLOBAL_SAWTOOTH_[% QUESTIONNAME() %]_SETTINGS.errorMessageSettings.minimumChecks.replace(/\[MIN(IMUM)?\]/ig, minimumChecks));
};
var addMinimumCharactersErrorMessageToQuestion = function(question, minimumCharacters) {
addErrorMessageToQuestion(question, GLOBAL_SAWTOOTH_[% QUESTIONNAME() %]_SETTINGS.errorMessageSettings.minimumCharacters.replace(/\[MIN(IMUM)?\]/ig, minimumCharacters));
};
var addErrorMessageToQuestion = function(question, errorMessage, isMissingAnswer) {
error = true;
var qdiv = $('#' + question + '_div');
$(qdiv).addClass('error_quest_highlight_branching');
var questionErrorBox = $(qdiv).find('.question_error_box_branching');
if (!$(questionErrorBox).length) {
questionErrorBox = $(' ');
$(qdiv).prepend($(questionErrorBox));
}
$(questionErrorBox).append(' ' + errorMessage + ' ');
};
var addGridRowErrorVariableHighlight = function(element) {
var closest = $(element).closest('.mobile_grid_card');
if ($(closest).length) {
$(closest).addClass('error_var_highlight_branching');
}
else {
closest = $(element).closest('tr');
$(closest).children().addClass('error_var_highlight_center_branching');
$(closest).children(':first-child').addClass('error_var_highlight_left_branching');
$(closest).children(':last-child').addClass('error_var_highlight_right_branching');
}
addErrorVariableHighlightToDescendents(closest);
};
var addGridColumnErrorVariableHighlight = function(element) {
var closest = $(element).closest('.mobile_grid_card');
if ($(closest).length) {
$(closest).addClass('error_var_highlight_branching');
}
else {
var index = $(element).closest('td').index() + 1;
closest = $(element).closest('tbody').find('> tr > td:nth-child(' + index + ')');
$(closest).addClass('error_var_highlight_middle_branching');
$(closest).first().addClass('error_var_highlight_top_branching');
$(closest).last().addClass('error_var_highlight_bottom_branching');
}
addErrorVariableHighlightToDescendents(closest);
};
var addErrorVariableHighlightToDescendents = function(element) {
addErrorVariableHighlight($(element).find('input:not(.total), textarea, select'));
};
var addErrorVariableHighlight = function(element) {
$(element).addClass('error_var_highlight_branching');
};
// Run verification
GLOBAL_SAWTOOTH_[% QUESTIONNAME() %]_SETTINGS.branchings.forEach(function(branch){
if (branch.requireResponse && branch.condition()) {
var question = branch.dependentQuestion;
var qdiv = $('#' + question + '_div');
if ($(qdiv).hasClass('select')) {
verifySelectQuestion(question, branch.selectMinimum);
}
else if ($(qdiv).hasClass('numeric')) {
verifyNumericQuestion(question);
}
else if ($(qdiv).hasClass('openend')) {
verifyOpenEndQuestion(question, branch.openEndMinimum);
}
else if ($(qdiv).hasClass('constantsum')) {
verifyConstantSumQuestion(question);
}
else if ($(qdiv).hasClass('ranking')) {
verifyRankingQuestion(question);
}
else if ($(qdiv).hasClass('semanticdiff')) {
verifySemanticDiffQuestion(question);
}
else if ($(qdiv).hasClass('grid')) {
verifyGridQuestion(question, branch.gridMinimums);
}
else if ($(qdiv).hasClass('freeformat')) {
verifyFreeFormatQuestion(question, branch.freeFormatMinimums);
}
}
});
if (error) {
strErrorMessage = '.';
}

{
	if ($i<=5) {if (LISTHASPARENTMEMBER("AttCheckAnsCons1",$i)) {ADD("AttCheckList",1,5);}}
	elsif ($i<=10) {if (LISTHASPARENTMEMBER("AttCheckAnsCons1",$i)) {ADD("AttCheckList",6,10);}}
	elsif ($i<=15) {if (LISTHASPARENTMEMBER("AttCheckAnsCons1",$i)) {ADD("AttCheckList",11,15);}}
	elsif ($i<=20) {if (LISTHASPARENTMEMBER("AttCheckAnsCons1",$i)) {ADD("AttCheckList",16,20);}}
	elsif ($i<=25) {if (LISTHASPARENTMEMBER("AttCheckAnsCons1",$i)) {ADD("AttCheckList",21,25);}}
	elsif ($i<=30) {if (LISTHASPARENTMEMBER("AttCheckAnsCons1",$i)) {ADD("AttCheckList",26,30);}}
}

{
	if ($i<=5) {if (LISTHASPARENTMEMBER("AttCheckAnsCons2",$i)) {ADD("AttCheckList",1,5);}}
	elsif ($i<=10) {if (LISTHASPARENTMEMBER("AttCheckAnsCons2",$i)) {ADD("AttCheckList",6,10);}}

Begin Unverified Perl
###Sure Değiştir
my $sure=9;

##Attention Check
my $maxFail=0;
my $cquest="AttCheck1,AttCheck2";
my $cnt=0;
my $totfail=0;
my $md=0;
my $reason="";
SETVALUE("QCR",$reason);

foreach my $cqst (split(/,/,$cquest)) {
    $cnt=$cnt+1;
	$maxFail=$maxFail+50;
    $md=MID(LISTVALUESARRAY("AttCheckAnsCons".$cnt), 2, length(LISTVALUESARRAY("AttCheckAnsCons".$cnt)) - 2);
	
    if (VALUE($cqst)!=$md && VALUE($cqst)!=0) {
        if ($cnt==2) 
		{
			$totfail=$totfail+100;
		} else 
	    {
			$totfail=$totfail+50;
		}
		$reason=$reason.",AttCheck".$cnt;
	}
}
####################################################################################################################
##Grid Check-TEK CEVAPLI SKALALI GRID Kontrolü 
##Kontrol edilecek sorular aşağıdaki gibi listleri ile birlikte virgülle tanımlanacak $quest="XX,YY..." ve $list="XXList,YYList..." gibi. Her sorunun listesi ayrı eklenmeli.
##Loop grid varsa $Lquest="XX,YY...", $LGList="ZZ,AA" ve $LoopList="ZZ,AA" atamalarını yapın.
##Kontrol için eklenecek grid yoksa değişkenleri boş bırakın. 

################### DEĞİŞTİR ##########################
##Grid
my $quest = ""; ##Grid soruları ekle
my $list = ""; ##Grid soruların listelerini ekle

##Loop Grid
my $Lquest = ""; ##LOOP Grid soruları ekle
my $LGlist = ""; ##LOOP Grid soruların listelerini ekle
my $LoopList = ""; ##LOOP Listelerini ekle
#######################################################

my $fail=0;
my $qlist="";
my $llist="";
$cnt=0;
my $rowval=0;
foreach my $qst (split(/,/, $Lquest))
{
	$qlist="";
	$llist ="";
	$qlist = (split(/,/, $LGlist))[$cnt];
	$llist = (split(/,/, $LoopList))[$cnt];
	
	foreach my $lp (split(/,/, substr(LISTVALUESARRAY($llist), 1, -1)))
	{   
	    $maxFail=$maxFail+50;
		$fail=0;
		$rowval=0;
			
	    $rowval = VALUE($qst."_r".LISTVALUE($qlist, 1).".".$lp);
	
		foreach my $i (split(/,/, substr(LISTVALUESARRAY($qlist), 1, -1)))
		{
			if ($rowval!=VALUE($qst."_r".$i.".".$lp)) {
		        last;
		    } else {
		        $fail=$fail+1;
		    }
		}
		
	    if ($fail==LISTLENGTH($qlist)) {
	        $totfail=$totfail+50;
			$reason=$reason.",".$qst.".".$lp;
	    }
	}	
	$cnt=$cnt+1;
}

$cnt=0;

foreach my $qst (split(/,/, $quest))
{
    $maxFail=$maxFail+50;
	$fail=0;
	$rowval=0;
	$qlist="";
	
    $qlist = (split(/,/, $list))[$cnt];
	
    $rowval = VALUE($qst."_r".LISTVALUE($qlist, 1));
	foreach my $i (split(/,/, substr(LISTVALUESARRAY($qlist), 1, -1)))
	{
		if ($rowval!=VALUE($qst."_r".$i)) {
	        last;
	    } else {
	        $fail=$fail+1;
	    }
	}
	
    
    if ($fail==LISTLENGTH($qlist)) {
        $totfail=$totfail+50;
		$reason=$reason.",".$qst;
    }
	
	$cnt=$cnt+1;
}
  
my $duration= GETVALUE ("timeDK");
if ($duration<$sure)
{
	$maxFail=$maxFail+150;
	$totfail=$totfail+150;
	$reason=$reason.",SURE=".$duration;
}

my $tp=TOTALPAGES();
for (my $page=1 ;$page<=$tp ;$page++)
{
	if (PAGETIME($page)>0 && PAGETIME($page)<=5)
	{
	   	##$reason=$reason.",HG-".$page;
	}
}

SETVALUE("QualityCheck_r1_c1",$totfail);
SETVALUE("QCR",$reason);

if ($totfail>100)
{
	SETVALUE("QCR","İPTAL".$reason);
}elsif ($totfail >= 50 && $totfail<=100){
	SETVALUE("QCR","KONTROL".$reason);
}

End Unverified

	    } else {
	        $fail=$fail+1;
	    }
	}
	
    
    if ($fail==LISTLENGTH($qlist)) {
        $totfail=$totfail+50;
		$reason=$reason.",".$qst;
    }
	
	$cnt=$cnt+1;
}
  
my $duration= GETVALUE ("timeDK");
if ($duration<$sure)
{
	$maxFail=$maxFail+150;
	$totfail=$totfail+150;
	$reason=$reason.",SURE=".$duration;
}

my $tp=TOTALPAGES();
for (my $page=1 ;$page<=$tp ;$page++)
{
	if (PAGETIME($page)>0 && PAGETIME($page)<=5)
	{
	   	##$reason=$reason.",HG-".$page;
	}
}

SETVALUE("QualityCheck_r1_c1",$totfail);
SETVALUE("QCR",$reason);

if ($totfail>100)
{
	SETVALUE("QCR","İPTAL".$reason);
}elsif ($totfail >= 50 && $totfail<=100){
	SETVALUE("QCR","KONTROL".$reason);
}

End Unverified

List Name: QualityCheckCons
===========================
Type: Constructed
Parent List: dummy
---------------------------

[Logic]:
ADD(dummy)
SetValue(QualityCheck_r1_c1,0)
SetValue(QCR,"-")
Begin Unverified Perl
###Sure Değiştir
my $sure=9;

##Attention Check
my $maxFail=0;
my $cquest="AttCheck1,AttCheck2";
my $cnt=0;
my $totfail=0;
my $md=0;
my $reason="";
SETVALUE("QCR",$reason);

foreach my $cqst (split(/,/,$cquest)) {
    $cnt=$cnt+1;
	$maxFail=$maxFail+50;
    $md=MID(LISTVALUESARRAY("AttCheckAnsCons".$cnt), 2, length(LISTVALUESARRAY("AttCheckAnsCons".$cnt)) - 2);
	
    if (VALUE($cqst)!=$md && VALUE($cqst)!=0) {
        if ($cnt==2) 
		{
			$totfail=$totfail+100;
		} else 
	    {
			$totfail=$totfail+50;
		}
		$reason=$reason.",AttCheck".$cnt;
	}
}
####################################################################################################################
##Grid Check-TEK CEVAPLI SKALALI GRID Kontrolü 
##Kontrol edilecek sorular aşağıdaki gibi listleri ile birlikte virgülle tanımlanacak $quest="XX,YY..." ve $list="XXList,YYList..." gibi. Her sorunun listesi ayrı eklenmeli.
##Loop grid varsa $Lquest="XX,YY...", $LGList="ZZ,AA" ve $LoopList="ZZ,AA" atamalarını yapın.
##Kontrol için eklenecek grid yoksa değişkenleri boş bırakın. 

################### DEĞİŞTİR ##########################
##Grid
my $quest = ""; ##Grid soruları ekle
my $list = ""; ##Grid soruların listelerini ekle

##Loop Grid
my $Lquest = ""; ##LOOP Grid soruları ekle
my $LGlist = ""; ##LOOP Grid soruların listelerini ekle
my $LoopList = ""; ##LOOP Listelerini ekle
#######################################################

my $fail=0;
my $qlist="";
my $llist="";
$cnt=0;
my $rowval=0;
foreach my $qst (split(/,/, $Lquest))
{
	$qlist="";
	$llist ="";
	$qlist = (split(/,/, $LGlist))[$cnt];
	$llist = (split(/,/, $LoopList))[$cnt];
	
	foreach my $lp (split(/,/, substr(LISTVALUESARRAY($llist), 1, -1)))
	{   
	    $maxFail=$maxFail+50;
		$fail=0;
		$rowval=0;
			
	    $rowval = VALUE($qst."_r".LISTVALUE($qlist, 1).".".$lp);
	
		foreach my $i (split(/,/, substr(LISTVALUESARRAY($qlist), 1, -1)))
		{
			if ($rowval!=VALUE($qst."_r".$i.".".$lp)) {
		        last;
		    } else {
		        $fail=$fail+1;
		    }
		}
		
	    if ($fail==LISTLENGTH($qlist)) {
	        $totfail=$totfail+50;
			$reason=$reason.",".$qst.".".$lp;
	    }
	}	
	$cnt=$cnt+1;
}

$cnt=0;

foreach my $qst (split(/,/, $quest))
{
    $maxFail=$maxFail+50;
	$fail=0;
	$rowval=0;
	$qlist="";
	
    $qlist = (split(/,/, $list))[$cnt];
	
    $rowval = VALUE($qst."_r".LISTVALUE($qlist, 1));
	foreach my $i (split(/,/, substr(LISTVALUESARRAY($qlist), 1, -1)))
	{
		if ($rowval!=VALUE($qst."_r".$i)) {
	        last;
	    } else {
	        $fail=$fail+1;
	    }
	}
	
    
    if ($fail==LISTLENGTH($qlist)) {
        $totfail=$totfail+50;
		$reason=$reason.",".$qst;
    }
	
	$cnt=$cnt+1;
}
  
my $duration= GETVALUE ("timeDK");
if ($duration<$sure)
{
	$maxFail=$maxFail+150;
	$totfail=$totfail+150;
	$reason=$reason.",SURE=".$duration;
}

my $tp=TOTALPAGES();
for (my $page=1 ;$page<=$tp ;$page++)
{
	if (PAGETIME($page)>0 && PAGETIME($page)<=5)
	{
	   	##$reason=$reason.",HG-".$page;
	}
}

SETVALUE("QualityCheck_r1_c1",$totfail);
SETVALUE("QCR",$reason);

if ($totfail>100)
{
	SETVALUE("QCR","İPTAL".$reason);
}elsif ($totfail >= 50 && $totfail<=100){
	SETVALUE("QCR","KONTROL".$reason);
}

End Unverified

===========================
List Name: GRUPYASList
===========================
Type: Predefined
Number of Items: 4
---------------------------

1	18-24
2	25-34
3	35-44
4	45-55

===========================
List Name: GrupYasCons
===========================
Type: Constructed
Parent List: GRUPYASList
---------------------------

[Logic]:
Begin Unverified Perl
my $list=LISTLENGTH("GRUPYASList");
for (my $i=1; $i<=$list; $i++)
{
	my @arr=split(/-/,LISTLABEL("GRUPYASList",$i));
    if (@arr[1]!="")
    {
		for (my $age=@arr[0]; $age<=@arr[1]; $age++)
		{
			if (VALUE("ACIKYAS")==$age)
			{
				ADD("GRUPYASList",$i);
				last;
			}
		}
 	}
	if (TEXTEXISTS(@arr[0],"+") && MID(@arr[0],1,2) < VALUE("ACIKYAS") )
	{
		ADD("GRUPYASList",$i);	
		last;
	}
		
}
	
End Unverified
